ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: Balance Reversal Complaint
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p><span style="font-size:16px"><strong>Reversal from Extra Credit Given (Customer to Retailer Balance Reversal)</strong></span></p>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Request will be received through RTG Reversal Portal </span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">RTG Backend team will check available balance (should be more than Rs.20) </span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">RTG Backend will callback to customer for consent if Reversal amount is greater than Rs.500 </span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Greater than Rs.500 reversal will be processed with customer consent or if no contact with customer after 1 attempt </span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">RTG Backend CCR will retrieve reversal amount or available balance (whichever is low) through CSRTB</span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">RTG Backend CCR will process posting through CPS Bulk within 4 Hours </span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Retailers will be informed via SMS where reversal not processed due to Low balance in customer account </span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">For C/O DO or Master reversal complaints, consent call is not required</span></li>
</ul>

Submission Channel: 1046
Escalation Level: I don't have updated information about this.
Created By: shahid.mehmood
Type (SOP/Complaint): Complaint
Verification Status: 18
Point of Contact: I don't have updated information about this.
Frequently Asked Questions: I don't have updated information about this.
Service Request Activity: I don't have updated information about this.
Checklist Items: <ul>
	<li>EVC Transaction Details</li>
</ul>

Required Questions: I don't have updated information about this.
Important Points: <ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Back office agent need to call the customer where reversal amount is &gt;500 for taking the consent &amp; process the request according to customer consent/response </span>
	<ul>
		<li><span style="font-size:14px">if customer&nbsp;not picked the call&nbsp;agent need to&nbsp;close the activity without taking action mentioning&nbsp;remarks</span></li>
	</ul>
	</li>
</ul>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Back office Agent will not&nbsp;send any ISMS to the customers where reversal amount is &lt;500</span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Back office agent will send the ISMS to retailer in both scenarios where amount is posting or not in order to close the loop of retailer complaint</span></li>
</ul>

Category: Prepaid

Complaint Description: <p>In case retailer is facing issues/complaint&nbsp;from his DO (Distribution Officer) and retailer calls at 1344 and compliant about DO service related issue we will guide retailer to launch the complaint from *510# self-services only</p>

<p><strong>Step by Step Self Service Procedure:</strong></p>

<p><strong>Step-1: </strong>Dial *510#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p><strong>Step-2: </strong>*510# menu pop up screen will appear with all available options &ldquo; Select Option 8 in menu Complaint&rdquo;</p>

<p><strong>Step-3: </strong>Retailer needs to select the type of complaint he is facing along with the number</p>

<p><strong>Step-4: </strong>Retailer needs to enter his PIN in order to verify that he is the original customer who is complaining</p>

<p><strong>Step-5: </strong>Retailer needs to mention his name</p>

<p><strong>Step-6: </strong>Retailer needs to mention his address (Shop address) &nbsp;</p>

<p><strong>Step-7: </strong>Complaint logged successfully along with confirmation message</p>

<h2>Process at Call Center-1344</h2>

<ul>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Franchise/ Retailer/Master line call at 1344, and request to change his CPS password</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Verify customer as per above verifications.</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Go to CPS and initiate auto completed &ldquo;<u>Reset Password</u>&rdquo; task, mention L3 in CPS notes</span></span></li>
	<li><span style="font-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif">Before closing it is mandatory to tell customer that &ldquo;this will be temporary password&nbsp; you need to change ASAP once you receive&rdquo; and close the call.</span></span></li>
</ul>

Required Questions: I don't have updated information about this.
Important Points: <ul>

Frequently Asked Questions: <p><strong>Q-How much time will it take to receive Debit Card?</strong></p>

<p>Customer will get Debit card in 15 working days.</p>

<p><strong>Q-If I already have a Debit Card, can I get another Debit Card?</strong></p>

<p>You will be able to place another order after 20 working days of your first order. Or in case your first order was rejected, you will be able to place another order immediately after order rejection.</p>

<p><strong>Q-How can a customer set Debit Card PIN?</strong></p>

<p>Customer can set card PIN via Mobile App, USSD or contact center</p>

<p><strong>Q-What is the commission structure and qualification criteria on debit card ordering?</strong></p>

<p>Retailer will get commission of PKR 50 once debit card is processed &amp; dispatched to customer.</p>

<p><strong>Q-How much time will it take for retailer to receive his commission?</strong></p>

<p>Retailer will receive his commission on monthly basis.</p>

<p><strong>Q-Is commission level same for both PayPak &amp; Master cards?</strong></p>

<p>Yes, Retailer to get same commission of PKR 50 on both debit cards.</p>

<p><strong>Q-Will retailer qualify for commission once customer debit is ordered?</strong></p>

<p>No, Retailer will qualify for commission once debit card is dispatched</p>

ðŸ“‹ ENTRY: Retailer Bundle upsell Failed (Multiple Attempts) - 1344
------------------------------------------------------------
Main Header: RTG
Network Provider: Jazz
Complaint Description: <p><span style="font-size:18px"><strong>Retailer Bundle upsell Failure (*964#)</strong></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:14px">From now onward if retailer attempt to subscribe bundle and failure occurs without any notification, However on multiple attempts bundle subscribed but amount deducted from retailer account on each attempt. In this case below mentioned process will be followed for better customer experience. </span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:14px">Please handle customer accordingly.</span></p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p><span style="font-size:14px"><strong>Reversal of Extra Posted Amount Due to Bundle Failure (Multiple Attempts)</strong></span></p>

<p><span style="font-size:14px"><strong>&nbsp;Retailer activate bundle but failed and amount posted in customer account (IN) without any notification</strong></span></p>

<ul style="list-style-type:disc">
	<li><span style="font-size:14px">Retailer re-attempt and bundle subscribed</span></li>
